15 Aug 2024, 00:00

Special forces of the Nigerian Air Force (NAF) on anti banditry operations in Zamfara State have killed two bandits and injured several others who fled with gunshot wounds. NAF Director of Public Relations and Information, Air Commodore Ibikunle Daramola, disclosed this in a statement today. Naija News understands that the ongoing anti-banditry operations is not limited to Zamfara state but also, Katsina, Kaduna, and other troubled states. According to Daramola, the bandits were killed following intelligence report that high-profile armed bandits were gathering around Rafi and Doka villages in Mada district in Gusau Local Government Area of the state.
